name:X‚Äçu‚Äçn‚Äçx‚Äçi‚Äça‚Äçn‚Äçg‚Äçl‚Äçe
info:Seascape Ocean View Pool Twin
info:Stayed in May 2024
info:Friends
info:73 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted June 7, 2024
msg:Location and transportation:
Located in Haitang Bay, it has its own coastline, but of course you can't go swimming in the sea.
Room view:
I booked a sea view suite with a private swimming pool. The pool in the room is spacious and you can play in the water. The scenery is really unbeatable. The balcony of the suite is big enough to have a party.
Room facilities:
The room facilities are complete, and fruits and champagne are delivered every day. I really can't finish the fruit. But the toiletries are fixed on the wall, which is very inconvenient. It's hard to squeeze when it's almost gone, so I suggest you adjust it.
The bathtub is a distance from the bathroom, which makes the whole room wet. Haha
Breakfast:
The breakfast is semi-buffet, and the food is quite rich. The opening time is also relatively late, so you can eat it as brunch. You can also eat local specialty noodles.
Gym:
I like the gym very much. The equipment is very clean and new, but it would be better if the equipment is more complete.
Swimming pool:
The opening time of the swimming pool is a bit unreasonable. I couldn't swim in both pools later in the evening. The scenery and comfort of the infinity pool are amazing.
Service:
Special thanks to Ryan for taking care of me during my stay and taking the trouble to meet my needs. I felt very at home.
If you want to come to Sanya for a vacation, I highly recommend the Rosewood Hotel. I will come again.

    In short, it is not recommended to live on vacation, especially for single ladies. Or friends who are very private. Let's start talking about the questions. To be honest, there are too many questions. Let's pick a few important ones.
    1. Not paying attention to the safety of residents. I checked in by myself on April 29 (I am a woman), and my husband came to see me the next day. (This is just my guess) There must be loopholes in the system and the professionalism of the service. Others are at least forty minutes or more. I forgot to bring my room card after swimming, and ran to the first floor wet in my swimsuit to ask for help to open the door. The service staff on the first floor asked me to go to the 14th floor to replace the room card.
  3. When you complain to customer service, they basically ignore it. I reported the problem to the room sales and duty manager and the room sales offered to send me some nightly snacks which were not delivered. The next day I said you could send a coconut to my room. I went out at 10 am and went back at 4 pm and didn't see it. This kind of arrogant service attitude is simply unheard of.
   Fourth, there are various details. There are many flaws in the hardware, and the quilt is always wet. (I have been to Madai twice, as well as Bali, and Banyan Tree Sanya, etc. The quilts are all dry. So the island is not the reason.) There are many small bugs in the room and restaurant. The internal structure of the hotel is very well separated from wet and dry, and the balcony is very large, which is suitable for ordering a late-night takeaway beer barbecue with sea breeze. The bedside table has unlimited charging is also a plus detail. The only embarrassment is that the TV and the bed are skewed. If you lie on the bed, don't watch TV. Your neck will be twisted. The fruit in the store is a bit shabby and there are only three apples. The breakfast is not too star-level.
Hotel facilities: The independent glass room on the first floor of the gym is great. The hotel's exclusive private beach can only be said to be okay. The waves are very big this season, just walk along the beach.
The overall check-in experience is still very good. There are many hotels in Sanya, and Rosewood's overall details and services are well done. It's worth it!
